[uBlock Origin 1.14.8+]
! Title: generic annoying stickybar filter
! Description: A generic list that makes annoying sticky headers unsticky
! Expires: 14 days
! Author: elypter
! Homepage: https://github.com/elypter/filter_processor/blob/master/generated_filterlists
! Support: https://github.com/elypter/filter_processor/blob/master/generated_filterlists/issues
! Download: https://raw.githubusercontent.com/elypter/filter_processor/master/generated_filterlists/blockhead(decoy_generic_selection).txt
! License: GPL-3.0

! Author: elypter
